### [1173] Screw Running Raw

**Tag path**  

`_dhm plc_/controller:global/plc_dryer_hwp_consumed/disc/disc_0_[7]`


**Historian / datatype**

- Historized tag ID: `1173`

- Ignition datatype code: `0` (numeric code from `sqlth_te.datatype`)

- Stored in the standard Ignition historian tables (surfaced via `unified_tag_values_view`).


**Usage in reporting views**

- `fire_dump_view` – Fire dump analysis: forward-fills diverter position, feed rate, moisture, and screw status tags, then integrates tons while the diverter sends material to screws.

- `rto_epd_report_view` – RTO EPD report: 15-minute nearest-sample state for RTO status, dryer metering bin status, and 3-hour average temperature, plus bypass/excursion flags.

- `wesp_epd_report_view` – WESP EPD report: 15-minute nearest-sample state for WESP status, dryer metering bin status, and 3-hour rectifier average, with bypass/excursion flags.


**Other names / labels**

- column aliases: `screw_running_raw`


**Notes**

- Boolean/on-off style tag used for equipment or system status in reports and dashboards.

**Other names / labels**

- commented names: `SBH DP 1`


**Notes**

### [8] Line 1 Shift Total

**Tag path**  

`_hwp pelleting line 1_/controller:global/line_1_shift_total`


**Historian / datatype**

- Historized tag ID: `8`

- Ignition datatype code: `1` (numeric code from `sqlth_te.datatype`)

- Stored in the standard Ignition historian tables (surfaced via `unified_tag_values_view`).


**Usage in reporting views**

- `shift_total_view` – Shift-level total tonnage: classifies samples into day/night shifts, picks a last-hour snapshot per shift and tag, adjusts Tag 1 with an assumed rate for a bad window, and outputs short/metric tons.

- `ytd_metric_total_view` – Year-to-date metric tonnage: shift-based max tonnage counters for tags 1, 8, and 9, converted to metric tons and accumulated with a manual starting offset.


**Notes**

- General-purpose historized tag. Add process-specific notes here if there are operating caveats or logic details.
